startMs);\n66:             } catch (WakeupException | InterruptException e) {\n67:                 throw e;\n68:             } catch (Exception e) {\n69:                 log.error(\n70:                     \"User provided listener {} failed on invocation of onPartitionsAssigned for partitions {}\",\n71:                     listener.get().getClass().getName(),\n72:                     assignedPartitions,\n73:                     e\n74:                 );\n75:                 return e;\n76:             }\n77:         }\n78: \n79:         return null;\n80:     }\n81: \n82:     public Exception invokePartitionsRevoked(final SortedSet<TopicPartition> revokedPartitions) {\n83:         log.info(\"Revoke previously assigned partitions {}\", revokedPartitions);\n84:         Set<TopicPartition> revokePausedPartitions = subscriptions.pausedPartitions();\n85:         revokePausedPartitions.retainAll(revokedPartitions);\n86:         if (!revokePausedPartitions.isEmpty())\n87:             log.info(\"The pause flag in partitions {} will be removed due to revocation.\", revokePausedPartitions);\n88: \n89:         Optional<ConsumerRebalanceListener> listener = subscriptions.rebalanceListener();\n90: \n91:         if (listener.isPresent()) {\n92:             try {\n93:                 final long startMs = time.milliseconds();\n94:                 listener.get().onPartitionsRevoked(revokedPartitions);\n95:                 metricsManager.recordPartitionsRevokedLatency(time.milliseconds() - StreamsRebalanceData (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/StreamsRebalanceData.java): A data holder class containing all information needed for Streams group rebalance protocol participation, including process ID, endpoint, subtopologies, reconciled task assignments, and partition distribution across hosts.\\n\\n5. StreamsRebalanceListener (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/StreamsRebalanceListener.java): An interface defining callbacks for Streams group rebalance events (task revocation, task assignment, and total task loss).\\n\\n**Event Classes (events/ subdirectory):**\\n\\n6.
